+                   -w "\nHTTP_STATUS:%{http_code}" \
+                   "${headers[@]}" "$@" "$url")
+    
+    local curl_exit_code=$?
+    if [ $curl_exit_code -ne 0 ]; then
+        echo "CURL_ERROR: Curl komutu baÅŸarÄ±sÄ±z oldu (exit code $curl_exit_code)."
+        return 1
+    fi
+
+    local http_status
+    http_status=$(echo "$response" | tail -n 1 | sed 's/HTTP_STATUS://')
+    local content
+    content=$(echo "$response" | sed '$d')
+
+    if [[ "$http_status" -lt 200 || "$http_status" -gt 299 ]]; then
+        echo "API_ERROR: HTTP $http_status. YanÄ±t: $content"
+        return 1
